***zakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zakken.html>zakken</a> (1358)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*sacken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sackon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sakkōną</i>, further etymology unknown, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sag</i>. Found natively only in the West Germanic languages.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zakken.html>zakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall, to drop, to sink
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> gist <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zakt.html>zakt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:proces.html>proces</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bodem.html>bodem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kuip.html>kuip</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The yeast <b>sinks</b> during the process to the bottom of the tub.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down, to go down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, to flunk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gezakt.html>gezakt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> rijexamen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>failed</b> my driving test.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to calm down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zakken.html>zakken</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rusteloos.html>rusteloos</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Could you <b>calm down</b> for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>? You're so restless.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***zakkenroller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zakkenroller.html>zakkenroller</a> (32872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zakkenrollen.html>zakkenrollen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> or from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zak.html>zak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pickpocket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">roller</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zalig.html>zalig</a> (5071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sālig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sēlīgaz</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sēliz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">selig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sillich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">silly</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seely</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sely</i>.

***zat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> (311)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sadaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zatter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">zatst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sated, full, especially with alcoholic beverage, i.e. drunk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> home <b>drunk</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dronken.html>dronken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>having <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> enough, having <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> it up to here, fed up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm <b>fed up</b> with this!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardappels.html>aardappels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still have <b>plenty</b> of potatoes here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> enough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wasmachine.html>wasmachine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kapot.html>kapot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaatwasser.html>vaatwasser</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's bad <b>enough</b> that my washing machine <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> broken, and now my dishwasher too!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***zaterdag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> (1891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">saterdach</i>, calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> Saturni</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Saterdag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">saterdei</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Saturday</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ze.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> (14)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">feminine singular subject</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <b>she</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sitting.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural subject</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <b>they</b> are sitting.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">feminine singular object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I see <b>her</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I see <b>them</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the Netherlands, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a reduced form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> chiefly when referring to feminine inanimate <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know the truth and didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> wish to know <b>it</b> either.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often avoided by using the reduced form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">h'<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>r</a></i> or the masculine form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a></i> or the neuter form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> or, in formal style, the full form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i>.</dd></dl>
<ul><li>In Belgium, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usual as a reduced form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> when referring to persons (as in the example further above).</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in certain short and idiomatic phrases in the imperative wishing one good luck, the most common by far being <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good luck at work!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a> (11113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*eciferus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">equiferus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The second sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebrapad.html>zebrapad</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebraatje.html>zebraatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></span>, a black-and-white striped equid of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a></i>; <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a> quagga</i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a> grevyi</i>. <span class="defdate">[from late 16th c.]</span></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a> crossing, a pedestrian crossing. <span class="defdate">[from mid 1950s.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebrapad.html>zebrapad</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zebrapad.html>zebrapad</a> (58469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pad.html>pad</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">path</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The choice of the element <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:zebra.html>zebra</a> crossing</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a> (1069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sêe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sēo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saiwiz</i>.

***zeehond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeehond.html>zeehond</a> (32870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seehont</i>. Synchronically equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hound, dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seehont</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seelhont</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seal-hound, seal-dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*selhaz</i>. Compare Low German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Saalhund</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>seal, any member of the family Phocidae

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeekoe.html>zeekoe</a> (58466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seecoe</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sea cow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

therefore [<a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>] let [someone] kill it with a shot straight in the front of the head, and let the people eat, because [it] <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> of a good taste, the milk running from the udders.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeekust.html>zeekust</a> (85845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kust.html>kust</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeekust.html>zeekust</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeekust.html>zeekusten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeekust.html>zeekustje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sea coast (marine shoreline) <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeeman.html>zeeman</a> (7897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seeman</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeeman.html>zeeman</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeemannen.html>zeemannen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeelui.html>zeelui</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeelieden.html>zeelieden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeeman.html>zeemannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A seaman, a male sailor.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***zeep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeep.html>zeep</a> (3656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seep</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sepe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sēpa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saipǭ</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">sepe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sjippe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Seife</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">soap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
